    CustomForm_DDCreateEquipment_Hull ^{
        Border=0,0,1024,767
        CodeBeforeRun ^{
            01=unknown arr0; int a=0, cnt=CT('DesignDepartmentModList.CreateEquipment.Hull',arr0), sub=0, add=0; str name='';
            02=for(a=0;a<cnt;a=a+1)
            03 ^{
                01=name=GetVariableName(arr0[a]);
